<h1 _ngcontent-pnu-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="navi（路径规划）"> navi（路径规划） </h1>

<div _ngcontent-pnu-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;"> <div><p>本模块提供路径规划功能。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p> <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 247px;"><h2 id="section164051883419" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">getDrivingRoutes<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section15371229153110" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getDrivingRoutes(params: DrivingRouteParams): Promise&lt;RouteResult&gt;</p> <p>规划两个地点之间的驾车路线。使用Promise异步回调。</p> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content"><ul><li>每次调用最多可以返回3条路径。</li><li>最多可以指定5个途经点。</li></ul> </div></div></div> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th id="mcps1.3.4.10.1.5.1.4" width="25.000000000000007%"><p><strong>说明</strong></p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="30.000000000000004%"><p>params</p> </td> <td width="10.000000000000002%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="25.000000000000007%"><p>驾车路径规划的参数。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p width="32.16%"><p>Promise&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-navi-api#section14125152320374">RouteResult</a>&gt;</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="67.84%"><p>Promise对象，返回<a device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">getDrivingRoutes<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getDrivingRoutes(context: common.Context, params: DrivingRouteParams): Promise&lt;RouteResult&gt;</p> <p>规划两个地点之间的驾车路线，支持传入Context上下文。使用Promise异步回调。</p> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content"><ul><li>每次调用最多可以返回3条路径。</li><li>最多可以指定5个途经点。</li></ul> </div></div></div> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本5.0.0(12)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> 2703px;"><h2 id="section13344132412116" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">getDrivingMatrix<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section13344132412116" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getDrivingMatrix(params: DrivingMatrixParams): Promise&lt;MatrixResult&gt;</p> <p>规划多个地点之间的驾车路线。使用Promise异步回调。</p> <p>该功能适用于高并发场景，例如网约车订单调度。在这种情况下，该功能可以计算多个起点和终点之间的路线，并找到网约车订单调度所需的起点和终点。</p> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content"><p>1. 只能在直线距离2000公里内规划驾车路线。</p> <p>2. 起点的数量乘以终点的数量不能超过100。</p> </div></div></div> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th id="mcps1.3.11.11.1.5.1.4" width="49.370000000000005%"><p><strong>说明</strong></p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="15.110000000000001%"><p>params</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="28.29%"><p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-navi-api#section28063259547">DrivingMatrixParams</a></p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.23%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="49.370000000000005%"><p>驾车批量算路的参数。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p class="msonormal"><strong>返回值：</strong></p>  <div <p>规划多个地点之间的驾车路线，支持传入Context上下文。使用Promise异步回调。</p> <p>该功能适用于高并发场景，例如网约车订单调度。在这种情况下，该功能可以计算多个起点和终点之间的路线，并找到网约车订单调度所需的起点和终点。</p> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div 2679px;"><h2 id="section99212131124" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">getWalkingMatrix<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section99212131124" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getWalkingMatrix(params: MatrixParams): Promise&lt;MatrixResult&gt;</p> <p>规划多个地点之间的步行路线。使用Promise异步回调。</p> <p>该功能适用于高并发场景，例如包裹递送。在这种情况下，该功能可以计算多个起点和终点之间的路线，并找到包裹递送所需的起点和终点。</p> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content"><p>1. 只能在直线距离150公里内规划步行路线。</p> <p>2. 起点的数量乘以终点的数量不能超过100。</p> </div></div></div> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th id="mcps1.3.13.11.1.5.1.4" width="49.370000000000005%"><p><strong>说明</strong></p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="15.110000000000001%"><p>params</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="28.29%"><p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-navi-api#section169321223144714">MatrixParams</a></p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.23%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="49.370000000000005%"><p>步行批量算路的参数。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p class="msonormal"><strong>返回值：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">getCyclingMatrix<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section20522154810218" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getCyclingMatrix(params: MatrixParams): Promise&lt;MatrixResult&gt;</p> <p>规划多个地点之间的骑行路线。使用Promise异步回调。</p> <p>该功能适用于高并发场景，例如包裹递送。在这种情况下，该功能可以计算多个起点和终点之间的路线，并找到包裹递送所需的起点和终点。</p> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content"><p>1. 只能在直线距离500公里内规划骑行路线。</p> <p>2. 起点的数量乘以终点的数量不能超过100。</p> </div></div></div> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.15.11.1.5.1.1" width="15.110000000000001%"><p><strong>参数名</strong></p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.15.11.1.5.1.2" width="28.29%"><p><strong>类型</strong></p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.15.11.1.5.1.3" width="7.22%"><p>必填</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.15.11.1.5.1.4" width="49.38%"><p><strong>说明</strong></p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="15.110000000000001%"><p>params</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="28.29%"><p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-navi-api#section169321223144714">MatrixParams</a></p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.22%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="49.38%"><p>骑行批量算路的参数。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p class="msonormal"><strong>返回值：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" width="67.84%"><p>Promise对象，返回<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-navi-api#section39821913105112">MatrixResult</a>。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">snapToRoads<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section36176371320" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>snapToRoads(params: SnapToRoadsParams): Promise&lt;SnapToRoadsResult&gt;</p> <p>基于指定的坐标点捕获道路，将用户轨迹移动到正确的道路，并返回车辆行驶在实际道路上的一组坐标点。使用Promise异步回调。</p> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content"><p>坐标点的数量不能超过100，并且两个相邻点之间的距离必须小于等于500米。</p> </div></div></div> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="49.370000000000005%"><p>轨迹绑路的参数。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p class="msonormal"><strong>返回值：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div 1248px;"><h2 id="section126101118153712" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">RouteCoordinate<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section126101118153712" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>路线规划属性。</p> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.7.1.6.1.1" width="30%"><p><strong>名称</strong></p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.7.1.6.1.2" width="25%"><p><strong>类型</strong></p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.7.1.6.1.3" width="7.08%"><p>只读</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.7.1.6.1.4" width="6.6000000000000005%"><p>可选</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.7.1.6.1.5" width="31.319999999999997%"><p><strong>说明</strong></p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="30%"><p>matchType</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><p>number</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.08%"><p>否</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.6000000000000005%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.319999999999997%"><p>起终点绑路类型。</p> <p>取值包括0、1、3，默认值为0。</p> <ul><li>0：限制绑路。起点避免绑定封闭、施工、限行、偏好设置所避免的道路，终点避免绑定高速、轮渡、 偏好设置所避免的道路。</li><li>1：无限制绑路，不考虑道路本身限制。</li><li>3：轨迹绑路，通过origins字段输入连续轨迹点的经纬度进行无限制绑路，只支持起点。</li></ul> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="30%"><p>latitude</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><p>number</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.08%"><p>否</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.6000000000000005%"><p>否</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.319999999999997%"><p>纬度，取值范围：[-90, 90] 。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="30%"><p>longitude</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><p>number</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.08%"><p>否</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.6000000000000005%"><p>否</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.319999999999997%"><p>经度，取值范围：[-180, 180) 。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="30%"><p>accuracy</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><p>number</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.08%"><p>否</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.6000000000000005%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.319999999999997%"><p>GPS定位精度，单位：米。无默认值。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="30%"><p>altitude</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><p>number</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.08%"><p>否</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.6000000000000005%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.319999999999997%"><p>海拔高度，单位：米。无默认值。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="30%"><p>bearing</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><p>number</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.08%"><p>否</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.6000000000000005%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.319999999999997%"><p>偏转角度。无默认值。</p> <p>以正北方向为0度、顺时针方向为正的角度，默认值为0，取值范围：[0, 360)。超出取值范围的值会换算成取值范围内的值，比如361会被换算成1，-1换算为359。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="30%"><p>speed</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><p>number</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.08%"><p>否</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.6000000000000005%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.319999999999997%"><p>当前行驶速度，单位：米/秒。无默认值。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="30%"><p>timestamp</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><p>number</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.08%"><p>否</p> </td> <td class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1617px;"><h2 id="section17987175793914" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">RouteParams<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" width="6.99%"><p>否</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.04%"><div class="p">目的地。<div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div width="31.04%"><p>表示指定计算路线的策略。取值包括：</p> <ul><li>0：速度快</li><li>1：避免收费</li><li>2：避免高速</li><li>4：距离短</li><li>8：避免轮渡</li><li>16：躲避拥堵</li><li>32：大路优先</li><li>64：智能路线</li><li>128：高速优先</li><li>256：少收费</li><li>512：速度流畅</li></ul> <p>默认值为0。</p> <p>步行和骑行仅支持两种策略：0和8。</p> <p>目前设置项16、32、128和256仅在中国大陆的路线规划中支持，后续将在其他国家和地区陆续支持这些设置项。</p> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content"><p>以上为单独策略，组合策略仅驾车支持1和8：避免收费+避免轮渡。</p> </div></div></div> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="28.349999999999998%"><p>extension</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" 驾车路线只能在直线距离2000公里内规划；步行路线只能在直线距离150公里内规划；骑行路线只能在直线距离500公里内规划。</p> <p>2. 起点的数量乘以终点的数量不能超过100。</p> </div></div></div> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="22.6%"><p>language</p> </td> <td <p>步行和骑行只支持两种设置项：0和8。</p> <p>驾车支持所有设置项，但目前设置项16、32、128和256仅在中国大陆的路线规划中支持，后续将在其他国家和地区陆续支持这些设置项。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div> <div class="tiledSection"
